	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TL_F-350/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TL_F-350/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

	-18,
	0,

	101,
	121
};


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TL_F-350/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TL_F-350/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				if v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = true;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = true;
				end
			end
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				if v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = false;
				end
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			if v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment') then
				v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
			else
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TL_F-350/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 Alt → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TL_F-350_Alt/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 Alt → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TL_F-350_Alt/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 Alt → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TL_F-350_Alt/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 Alt → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				if v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = true;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = true;
				end
			end
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				if v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = false;
				end
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			if v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment') then
				v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
			else
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;

		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TL_F-350_Boom/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern2.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern2 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 Boom → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)

	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)
	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9)
	local T10 = elsModule(ELSModel.T10)

	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.G1)
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2)
	local G3 = elsModule(ELSModel.G3)
	local G4 = elsModule(ELSModel.G4)
	local G5 = elsModule(ELSModel.G5)
	local G6 = elsModule(ELSModel.G6)
	
	--Front lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

	--Back lights lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
				F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));

				G1(1);
				G2(1);
				G3(0);
				G4(0);
				G5(1);
				G6(1);		
				wait(0.045)							
							
				G1(1);
				G2(0);
				G3(0);
				G4(1);
				G5(1);
				G6(1);		
				wait(0.045)							
							
				G1(0);
				G2(0);
				G3(1);
				G4(1);
				G5(1);
				G6(1);		
				wait(0.045)							
							
				G1(0);
				G2(1);
				G3(1);
				G4(1);
				G5(1);
				G6(1);		
				wait(0.045)							
					
					
				end
			end)
		end)()				
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
				R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
				R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
				R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));														
				wait(0.10)						
								
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.065)					
									
				R1(0);
				R2(0);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.10)						
								
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.065)							
										
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(0);
				R4(0);	
				wait(0.10)						
								
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.065)						
										
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(0);
				R4(0);	
				wait(0.10)						
								
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.065)						

				end
			end)
		end)()			

				
		
	else
		T1(1)
		T2(1)
		T3(1)
		T4(1)
		T5(1)
		T6(1)
		T7(1)
		T8(1)
		T9(1)
		T10(1)
		R1(1)
		R2(1)

		F1(1)

end


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TL_F-350_Boom/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 Boom → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TL_F-350_Boom/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 Boom → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 Boom → Config → Modules

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TL_F-350_Boom/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TL F-350 Boom → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				if v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = true;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = true;
				end
			end
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				if v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = false;
				end
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			if v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment') then
				v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
			else
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Taxi/TL_CV_Taxi/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Taxi → TL CV Taxi → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;

			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Taxi/TL_CV_Taxi/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Taxi → TL CV Taxi → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Taxi/TL_CV_Taxi/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Taxi → TL CV Taxi → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_Bus/CarServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    CarServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL Bus
    Parent: TL Bus
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
--[[local Knit = require(game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Knit);

Knit.OnStart():await();

require(Knit.Modules.Car).new(script.Parent, false);]]

game:GetService('ServerScriptService'):WaitForChild('AeroLoaded');

_G.Aero.Modules.Car.new(script.Parent, false);

local vehicleSeat = script.Parent.Chassis.VehicleSeat;

local lastPlayer;

vehicleSeat:GetAttributeChangedSignal('LastOccupant'):Connect(function()
	local occupant = vehicleSeat:GetAttribute('LastOccupant');
	
	if occupant ~= nil then
		local player = game.Players:FindFirstChild(occupant);
		if player then
			if player.Team.Name == 'Translink' then
				lastPlayer = player;
				_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(player, 'BusGuiVisibility', true);
			end
		end;
	elseif occupant == nil and lastPlayer then
		if lastPlayer:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then
			_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(lastPlayer, 'BusGuiVisibility', false);
		else
			lastPlayer = nil;
		end
	end;
end);


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_Bus/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL Bus → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	
	-- LIGHTBAR
	local F1 = ELSModel.F1;
	local F2 = ELSModel.F2;
	local F3 = ELSModel.F3;
	local F4 = ELSModel.F4;
	local F5 = ELSModel.F5;
	local F6 = ELSModel.F6;
	local F7 = ELSModel.F7;
	local F8 = ELSModel.F8;
	local F9 = ELSModel.F9;
	
	-- Front Lights
	local M1 = ELSModel.M1;
	local M2 = ELSModel.M2;
	local M3 = ELSModel.M3;
	local M4 = ELSModel.M4;
	
	-- Door Lights
	local G1 = ELSModel.G1;
	local G2 = ELSModel.G2;
	
	-- Tiny Lightbar Lights
	local A1 = ELSModel.A1;
	local A2 = ELSModel.A2;
	local A3 = ELSModel.A3;
	local A4 = ELSModel.A4;
	
	-- Back Lights
	local C1 = ELSModel.C1;
	local C2 = ELSModel.C2;
	local C3 = ELSModel.C3;
	local C4 = ELSModel.C4;
	local C5 = ELSModel.C5;
	local C6 = ELSModel.C6;
	local C7 = ELSModel.C7;
	local C8 = ELSModel.C8;
	
	-- Back Lights (actual back)

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_Bus/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL Bus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	headlightsState = script.Parent.Parent.State.Headlights.Value;
	
	print(headlightsState, enabled);

	if enabled and headlightsState then
		print('enabled and headlights');
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
		end;
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			if not v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Beam') then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
			end;
		end;
	elseif enabled and not headlightsState then
		print('enabled and no headlights');
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(196, 40, 28);
		end;
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			if not v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Beam') then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(196, 40, 28);
			end;
		end;
	elseif not enabled and not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(196, 40, 28);
		end;
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			if not v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Beam') then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(196, 40, 28);
			end;
		end;
	elseif not enabled and headlightsState then
		for _,v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(196, 40, 28);
		end;
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			if not v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Beam') then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_Bus/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL Bus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			if v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Beam') then
				v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			else
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			end;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			if v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Beam') then
				v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			else
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			end;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_Bus/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL Bus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_Bus/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL Bus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1); 
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2);

	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4);

	local Q1 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q1); 
	local Q2 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q2); 

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					T1(0, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
					T2(0, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));							
					T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));

					T3(1);
					T4(1);
					wait(0.12);

					T1(1);
					T2(1);
					T3(1);
					T4(1);
					wait(0.05);

					T1(1);
					T2(1);
					T3(0);
					T4(0);
					wait(0.12);

					T1(1);
					T2(1);
					T3(1);
					T4(1);
					wait(0.05);					

					T1(1);
					T2(1);
					T3(0);
					T4(0);
					wait(0.12);

					T1(1);
					T2(1);
					T3(1);
					T4(1);
					wait(0.05);						

				end
			end)
		end)()

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					R1(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
					R2(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));							
					
					R1(0);
					R2(0);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					wait(0.12);

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					wait(0.05);					

					R1(0);
					R2(0);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					wait(0.12);

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					wait(0.05);							

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(0);
					R4(0);
					wait(0.12);

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					wait(0.05);							

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(0);
					R4(0);
					wait(0.12);

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					wait(0.05);										
				end
			end)
		end)()		

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					Q1(0);
					Q2(1);
					wait(0.12);

					Q1(1);
					Q2(1);
					wait(0.05);					

					Q1(0);
					Q2(1);
					wait(0.12);

					Q1(1);
					Q2(1);
					wait(0.05);							

					Q1(1);

					wait(0.12);

					Q1(1);
					Q2(1);
					wait(0.05);						
				end
			end)
		end)()		


	else
		T1(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
		T2(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_Explorer/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_Explorer/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

		end

		ELSModel.TD2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);

		ELSModel.TD4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--[[
    CarServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL LFS Bus
    Parent: TL LFS Bus
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
--[[local Knit = require(game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Knit);

Knit.OnStart():await();

require(Knit.Modules.Car).new(script.Parent, false);]]

game:GetService('ServerScriptService'):WaitForChild('AeroLoaded');

_G.Aero.Modules.Car.new(script.Parent, false);

local vehicleSeat = script.Parent.Chassis.VehicleSeat;

local lastPlayer;

vehicleSeat:GetAttributeChangedSignal('LastOccupant'):Connect(function()
	local occupant = vehicleSeat:GetAttribute('LastOccupant');

	if occupant ~= nil then
		local player = game.Players:FindFirstChild(occupant);
		if player then
			lastPlayer = player;
			_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(player, 'BusGuiVisibility', true);
		end;
	elseif occupant == nil and lastPlayer:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then
		_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(lastPlayer, 'BusGuiVisibility', false);
	end;
end);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_LFS_Bus/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL LFS Bus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_LFS_Bus/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL LFS Bus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

	121

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_LFS_Bus/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL LFS Bus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_LFS_Bus/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL LFS Bus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_LFS_Bus/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL LFS Bus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_LFS_HEV/CarServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    CarServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL LFS HEV
    Parent: TL LFS HEV
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
--[[local Knit = require(game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Knit);

Knit.OnStart():await();

require(Knit.Modules.Car).new(script.Parent, false);]]

game:GetService('ServerScriptService'):WaitForChild('AeroLoaded');

_G.Aero.Modules.Car.new(script.Parent, false);

local vehicleSeat = script.Parent.Chassis.VehicleSeat;

local lastPlayer;

vehicleSeat:GetAttributeChangedSignal('LastOccupant'):Connect(function()
	local occupant = vehicleSeat:GetAttribute('LastOccupant');

	if occupant ~= nil then
		local player = game.Players:FindFirstChild(occupant);
		if player then
			lastPlayer = player;
			_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(player, 'BusGuiVisibility', true);
		end;
	elseif occupant == nil and lastPlayer:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then
		_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(lastPlayer, 'BusGuiVisibility', false);
	end;
end);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	
	-- LIGHTBAR
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4);
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5);

	local F7 = elsModule(ELSModel.F7);
	local F8 = elsModule(ELSModel.F8);

	local M2 = elsModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = elsModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = elsModule(ELSModel.M4);

	-- Door Lights
	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.G1);
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2);
	
	-- Back Lights
	local C1 = elsModule(ELSModel.C1);
	local C2 = elsModule(ELSModel.C2);
	local C3 = elsModule(ELSModel.C3);
	local C4 = elsModule(ELSModel.C4);
	local C5 = elsModule(ELSModel.C5);
	local C6 = elsModule(ELSModel.C6);
	local C7 = elsModule(ELSModel.C7);
	local C8 = elsModule(ELSModel.C8);

	local X2 = elsModule(ELSModel.X2);
	local X3 = elsModule(ELSModel.X3);
	local X4 = elsModule(ELSModel.X4);
	
	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					F5(1);
					F6(1);
					F7(1);
					F8(1);
					F9(1);
					wait(0.1);
				end
			end)
		end)()
			coroutine.wrap(function()
				pcall(function()
					while true do
						M1(1);
						M2(1);
						M3(1);
						M4(1);
						wait(0.1);
						M1(1);
						M2(1);
						M3(1);
						M4(1);
						wait(0.1);
				   end
			    end)
			end)()
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					G1(0);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.05);
					G1(1);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.05);
					G1(1);
					G2(0);
					wait(0.05);
					G1(1);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.05);
				end
			end)
		end)()
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					C1(1);
					C2(1);
					C3(0);
					C4(0);
					C5(1);
					C6(1);
					C7(0);
					C8(0);
					wait(0.2);
					C1(0);
					C2(0);
					C3(1);
					C4(1);
					C5(0);
					C6(0);
					C7(1);
					C8(1);
					wait(0.2);
				end
			end)
		end)()
		coroutine.wrap(function()

					X1(0);
					X2(1);
					X3(1);
					X4(1);
					wait(0.15);
					X1(0);
					X2(0);
					X3(1);
					X4(1);
					wait(0.15);
					X1(1);
					X2(0);
					X3(0);
					X4(1);
					wait(0.15);
					X1(1);

	else

		X2(1);
		X3(1);
		X4(1);

		C3(1);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_LFS_HEV/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL LFS HEV → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_LFS_HEV/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL LFS HEV → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_LFS_HEV/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL LFS HEV → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_LFS_HEV/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL LFS HEV → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Transit/TL_LFS_HEV/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Transit → TL LFS HEV → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/CDC/CDC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → CDC → CDC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/CDC/CDC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → CDC → CDC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/CDC/CDC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → CDC → CDC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights2;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = neonMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Material = neonMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = smoothMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Material = smoothMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/CDC/CDC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → CDC → CDC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/CDC/CDC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → CDC → CDC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/CDC/CDC_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → CDC → CDC Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/CDC/CDC_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → CDC → CDC Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/CDC/CDC_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → CDC → CDC Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/CDC/CDC_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → CDC → CDC Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/ICU/VCH_ICU_Explorer/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → ICU → VCH ICU Explorer → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local elsModule = script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart;

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local frontb = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.FrontB);
	local frontt = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.FrontT);
	local mirror = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.Mirror);
	local sidef = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.SideF);
	local sideb = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.SideB);
	local rear = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.Rear);
	local reverse = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.Reverse);
	
	local mainside = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.MainSide);
	local mainfront = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.MainFront);
	local mainrear = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.MainRear);
	
	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				frontb(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				frontt(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				mirror(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				sidef(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				sideb(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				rear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				reverse(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				mainside(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				mainfront(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				mainrear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					rear(0)
					mirror(0)
					reverse(1)
					mainrear(1)
					wait(0.45)
					rear(1)
					mirror(1)
					reverse(0)
					mainrear(0)
					wait(0.45)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				frontb(1)
				frontt(1)
				sidef(1)
				sideb(1)
				mainside(1)
				mainfront(1)
			end)
		end)()

	else
		frontb(1)
		frontt(1)
		mirror(1)
		sidef(1)
		sideb(1)
		rear(1)
		reverse(1)
		mainside(1)
		mainfront(1)
		mainrear(1)
	end
end

	local frontt = elsModule(ELSModel.FrontT);
	local mirror = elsModule(ELSModel.Mirror);
	local sidef = elsModule(ELSModel.SideF);
	local sideb = elsModule(ELSModel.SideB);
	local rear = elsModule(ELSModel.Rear);
	local reverse = elsModule(ELSModel.Reverse);
	
	local mainside = elsModule(ELSModel.MainSide);
	local mainfront = elsModule(ELSModel.MainFront);
	local mainrear = elsModule(ELSModel.MainRear);
	
	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					rear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					reverse(1)
					sideb(1)
					sidef(1)
					mirror(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					frontb(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.07)
					rear(1)
					reverse(1)
					sideb(1)
					sidef(1)
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.04)
					rear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					reverse(1)
					sideb(1)
					sidef(1)
					mirror(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					frontb(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.07)
					rear(1)
					reverse(1)
					sideb(1)
					sidef(1)
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.04)
					rear(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					reverse(1)
					sideb(1)
					sidef(1)
					mirror(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					frontb(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.07)
					rear(1)
					reverse(1)
					sideb(1)
					sidef(1)
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.04)
					rear(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					reverse(1)
					sideb(1)
					sidef(1)
					mirror(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					frontb(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.07)
					rear(1)
					reverse(1)
					sideb(1)
					sidef(1)
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.04)
					rear(1)
					reverse(0)
					sideb(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					sidef(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					wait(0.07)
					rear(1)
					reverse(1)
					sideb(1)
					sidef(1)
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.04)
					rear(1)
					reverse(0)
					sideb(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					sidef(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					wait(0.07)
					rear(1)
					reverse(1)
					sideb(1)
					sidef(1)
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.04)
					rear(1)
					reverse(0)
					sideb(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					sidef(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					wait(0.07)
					rear(1)
					reverse(1)
					sideb(1)
					sidef(1)
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.04)
					rear(1)
					reverse(0)
					sideb(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					sidef(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					wait(0.07)
					rear(1)
					reverse(1)
					sideb(1)
					sidef(1)
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.04)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					mainside(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					mainrear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1)
					mainrear(1)
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					mainrear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1)
					mainrear(1)

					mainside(0, Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255))
					mainrear(1, Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255))
					wait(0.07)

					mainrear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1)
					mainrear(1)
					wait(0.07)

			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					mainfront(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					wait(0.07)

		mainrear(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
	end
end


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/ICU/VCH_ICU_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → ICU → VCH ICU Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/ICU/VCH_ICU_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → ICU → VCH ICU Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/ICU/VCH_ICU_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → ICU → VCH ICU Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/ICU/VCH_ICU_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → ICU → VCH ICU Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/ICU/VCH_ICU_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → ICU → VCH ICU Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/ICU/VCH_ICU_Sprinter/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → ICU → VCH ICU Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end
