================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/ICU/VCH_ICU_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → ICU → VCH ICU Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights2;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = neonMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Material = neonMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = smoothMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Material = smoothMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/ICU/VCH_ICU_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → ICU → VCH ICU Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/ICU/VCH_ICU_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → ICU → VCH ICU Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → Medical Academy → VCH Academy Explorer → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local elsModule = script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart;

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local frontb = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.FrontB);
	local frontt = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.FrontT);
	local mirror = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.Mirror);
	local sidef = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.SideF);
	local sideb = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.SideB);
	local rear = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.Rear);
	local reverse = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.Reverse);
	
	local mainside = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.MainSide);
	local mainfront = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.MainFront);
	local mainrear = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.MainRear);
	
	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				frontb(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				frontt(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				mirror(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				sidef(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				sideb(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				rear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				reverse(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				mainside(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				mainfront(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				mainrear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					rear(0)
					mirror(0)
					reverse(1)
					mainrear(1)
					wait(0.45)
					rear(1)
					mirror(1)
					reverse(0)
					mainrear(0)
					wait(0.45)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				frontb(1)
				frontt(1)
				sidef(1)
				sideb(1)
				mainside(1)
				mainfront(1)
			end)
		end)()

	else
		frontb(1)
		frontt(1)
		mirror(1)
		sidef(1)
		sideb(1)
		rear(1)
		reverse(1)
		mainside(1)
		mainfront(1)
		mainrear(1)
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/Medical_Academy/VCH_Academy_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → Medical Academy → VCH Academy Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/Medical_Academy/VCH_Academy_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → Medical Academy → VCH Academy Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/Medical_Academy/VCH_Academy_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → Medical Academy → VCH Academy Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/Medical_Academy/VCH_Academy_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → Medical Academy → VCH Academy Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1);
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2);
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3);
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4);
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5);
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6);
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7);
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8);
	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9);
	local T10 = elsModule(ELSModel.T10);
	local S1 = elsModule(ELSModel.S1);
	local S2 = elsModule(ELSModel.S2);
	local S3 = elsModule(ELSModel.S3);
	local S4 = elsModule(ELSModel.S4);
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4);
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1);
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2);
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local D1 = elsModule(ELSModel.D1);
	local D2 = elsModule(ELSModel.D2);
	if enabled then
		task.defer(function()
			while true do	
				F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				F2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));

				R1(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				R2(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				S1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				S2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				S3(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				S4(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));		
				T1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));		
				T5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

				T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));

				T10(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				D1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				D2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				wait(0.3)
						
				T1(1)
				T2(1)
				T3(1)
				T4(1)			
				T5(1)
				T6(1)
				T7(1)
				T8(1)
				T9(1)
				T10(1)	
				F1(1)
				F2(1)
				F3(1)
				F4(1)	
				D1(1)
				D2(1)

				S2(1)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				R1(1)
				R2(1)
				R3(1)
				R4(1)
				wait(0.15)

				T1(0)

				T3(0)
				T4(0)			
				T5(0)
				T6(1)
				T7(1)

				F1(0)

				S4(0)
				R1(0)
				R2(0)
				R3(1)
				R4(1)
				wait(0.3)				

				T1(1)

			end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/Medical_Academy/VCH_Academy_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → Medical Academy → VCH Academy Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/Medical_Academy/VCH_Academy_Sprinter/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → Medical Academy → VCH Academy Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/Medical_Academy/VCH_Academy_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → Medical Academy → VCH Academy Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights2;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = neonMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Material = neonMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = smoothMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Material = smoothMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/Medical_Academy/VCH_Academy_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → Medical Academy → VCH Academy Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/Medical_Academy/VCH_Academy_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → Medical Academy → VCH Academy Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;
